CC   -!- DOMAIN: Has a modular structure: a carbohydrate-binding module

CC       terminal endo-1,4-mannanase catalytic module. The genes for
CC       catalytic modules and CBMs seem to have evolved separately and
CC       have been linked by gene fusion.

CC   -!- FUNCTION: Hydrolyzes 1,4-beta linked polysaccharide backbones of
CC       mannans, one of the major hemicellulose components in hardwoods
CC       and softwoods. Shows very high activity against mannohexaose but
CC       not against mannopentaose and smaller mannooligosaccharides. The
CC       major products released from mannooligosaccharide hydrolysis are
CC       mannose and mannobiose. The reiterated 40 AA domain is involved in
CC       binding the cellulase-hemicellulase complex.
CC   -!- CATALYTIC ACTIVITY: Random hydrolysis of (1->4)-beta-D-mannosidic
CC       linkages in mannans, galactomannans and glucomannans.
CC   -!- DOMAIN: Consists of a catalytic N-terminal domain linked to a
CC       reiterated non-catalytic C-terminal domain.
CC   -!- SIMILARITY: Belongs to the glycosyl hydrolase 26 family.
CC       {ECO:0000255|PROSITE-ProRule:PRU01100, ECO:0000305}.
CC   -!- SIMILARITY: Contains 3 CBM10 (carbohydrate binding type-10)
CC       domains. {ECO:0000255|PROSITE-ProRule:PRU01099, ECO:0000305}.
CC   -!- SIMILARITY: Contains 1 CBM6 (carbohydrate binding type-6) domain.
CC       {ECO:0000255|PROSITE-ProRule:PRU00523}.
CC   -!- SIMILARITY: Contains 1 GH26 (glycosyl hydrolase family 26) domain.
